# kali - setup desktop so we can rdp into the server and see the desktop

This is all for fun.  Use a kali vm for pen testing.

## Install on Windows10 with WSL

Go to Windows Store, and search Kali

```bash

Install Kail with 'Install'
Enter new UNIX usersname:
Eneter new UNIX password:
Retype new UNIX password:
 Installing, this may take a few minutes...
Please create a default UNIX user account. The username does not need to match your Windows username.
For more information visit: https://aka.ms/wslusers
Enter new UNIX username: acidburn
Enter new UNIX password:
Retype new UNIX password:
Sorry, passwords do not match
passwd: Authentication token manipulation error
passwd: password unchanged
Try again? [y/N] Y\
Enter new UNIX password:
Retype new UNIX password:
passwd: password updated successfully
Installation successful!
Launch
Setup user and pwd steps

```
## Install the Kali Desktop Environment



### Check for your version
```bash

$ cat etc/issue
$ Kali GNU/Linux Rolling \n \l

```
## Get the Desktop environment shellscript

```bash

$ wget https://kali.sh/xfce4.sh
htts://kali.sh/xfce4.sh: Unsupported scheme ‘htts’.
acidburn@coldflame:~$ wget https://kali.sh/xfce4.sh
--2018-05-24 08:37:55--  https://kali.sh/xfce4.sh
Resolving kali.sh (kali.sh)... 45.79.158.143
Connecting to kali.sh (kali.sh)|45.79.158.143|:443... connected.
HTTP request sent, awaiting response... 200 OK
Length: 315 [text/x-sh]
Saving to: ‘xfce4.sh’

xfce4.sh                      100%[=================================================>]     315  --.-KB/s    in 0s

2018-05-24 08:37:55 (3.41 MB/s) - ‘xfce4.sh’ saved [315/315]


```

### Give permissions to the script and run the script
